CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // Compute the absolute maximum of the atom in the thread group\n            // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale;\n            int encoding_scale;\n            decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // Convert from f16x2_t to uint16x2_t\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Pack 8 x q4 into int32_t\n            int qw = q[0] | (q[1] << 4) | (q[2] << 8) | (q[3] << 12);\n\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            int32_t* qw_ptr   = reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                    {\n                        int32_t q4 = ((qw >> (i * 4)) & kMask000F) | kHalf2_1024;\n                        w[i]       = packed_add<half>(q4, kHalf2_1032);\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        int32_t int16_2        = (qw >> (i * 4)) & kMask000F;\n __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n block-scaled Int3 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize. Uniform symmetric quantization (round-to-int + clip),\n// matching the structure of CodecQ4. Signed range is [-4, +3].\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecQ3 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Layout per quantization block (32 values = 8 threads * 4 fp16x2 lanes):\n    //  - each thread owns 8 values and writes:\n    //      * q2 payload : 8 * 2 bits -> uint16 (2 bytes)\n    //      * q1 payload : 8 * 1 bit  -> uint8  (1 byte)\n    //  - one scale is shared per 32 values and written by group leader.\n    //\n    // kRankTileStride is split as:\n    //   [0   .. 511] : q2 payload region (256 threads * 2 bytes)\n    //   [512 .. 767] : q1 payload region (256 threads * 1 byte)\n    //   [768 .. 895] : scale region (32 groups * 4 bytes)\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 896;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileQ1Offset        = 512;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 768;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // {-1/4.0h, -1/4.0h}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t. Sign-flipped so absmax maps\n    // to -4; the sign cancels with decoding_scale on the recv side.\n    static constexpr int kScaleFactor = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xB400B400 : 0xBE80BE80;\n\n    // {1e-7, 1e-7}, f16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleEpsilon = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7;\n\n    // {-4, -4}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMin = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xC400C400 : 0xC080C080;\n\n    // {+3, +3}, f16x2_t / bf16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMax = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x42004200 : 0x40404040;\n\n    // {+4, +4}, int16x2_t -- shifts signed [-4, +3] to unsigned [0, 7].\n    static constexpr int kRangeBias = 0x00040004;\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ3(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // 1) Per-group dynamic scale (shared across 32 values).\n            int wblockmax      = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // 2) Scale + clip to signed int3 range [-4, +3].\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // 3) Round to integer and bias to unsigned domain [0, 7].\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // 4) Split each 3-bit unsigned value into low-2-bit and high-1-bit\n            // halves, packed into one uint16 (low 2 bits per value) plus one\n            // uint8 (high 1 bit per value).\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            uint8_t q1w  = 0;\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    uint32_t v = static_cast<uint32_t>(tw[i]) & 0x7u;\n                    q2w |= static_cast<uint16_t>((v & 0x3u) << (i * 2));\n                    q1w |= static_cast<uint8_t>(((v >> 2) & 0x1u) << i);\n                }\n            }\n\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint8_t* q1w_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ1Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n            *q1w_ptr = q1w;\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint8_t* q1w_ptr  = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ1Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            uint8_t q1w  = *q1w_ptr;\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack unsigned values [0, 7] then shift back to signed domain\n            // [-4, +3] by adding kRangeMin.\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                int16_t qv[8];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    uint32_t low2  = (q2w >> (2 * i)) & 0x3u;\n                    uint32_t high1 = (q1w >> i) & 0x1u;\n                    qv[i]          = static_cast<int16_t>(low2 | (high1 << 2));\n                }\n\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    int qpack = packed_from_int16_pair<T>(qv[2 * i], qv[2 * i + 1]);\n                    w[i]      = packed_add<T>(qpack, kRangeMin);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decode scale to reconstruct fp16/bf16 lanes.\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Int6 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Int6 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecQ6 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a int6x8_t (4B + 2B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 1664;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileQ2Offset        = 1024;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 1536;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0,\n                  \"kRankTransmittedTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // Constants configuration\n\n    // {-1/32.0h, -1/32.0h}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleFactor = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xA800A800 : 0xBD00BD00;\n\n    // {1e-7, 1e-7}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kScaleEpsilon = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7;\n\n    // {-32, -32}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMin = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0xD000D000 : 0xC200C200;\n\n    // {+31, +31}, fp16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeMax = std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x4FC04FC0 : 0x41F841F8;\n\n    // {+32, +32}, int16x2_t\n    static constexpr int kRangeBias = 0x00200020;\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecQ6(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // Compute the absolute maximum of the atom in the thread group\n            // In 2 blocks of values, upper/lower halves of the f16x2_t\n            int wblockmax = group_abs_max<T>(atom);\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale;\n            int encoding_scale;\n            decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wblockmax, kScaleFactor);\n            encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            int32x4_t w;\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n                w[i] = packed_max<T>(w[i], kRangeMin);\n                w[i] = packed_min<T>(w[i], kRangeMax);\n            }\n\n            // Convert from f16x2_t to uint16x2_t\n            int32x4_t q;\n            {\n                int16_t* qi = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n                T* wh       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                    qi[i] = (int16_t)rintf(T2float_cast(wh[i]));\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    q[i] = packed_add<int16_t>(q[i], kRangeBias);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Pack 8 x q6 into int32_t + int16_t\n            uint32_t q4w;\n            uint16_t q2w = 0;\n            q4w = (q[0] & 0x000F000F) | ((q[1] & 0x000F000F) << 4) | ((q[2] & 0x000F000F) << 8) |\n                  ((q[3] & 0x000F000F) << 12);\n            {\n                int16_t* tw = reinterpret_cast<int16_t*>(&q);\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    q2w |= (tw[i] >> 4) << (i * 2);\n                }\n            }\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q4w, q4w_ptr);\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(q2w, q2w_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            uint32_t* q4w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            uint16_t* q2w_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint16_t*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileQ2Offset) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            uint32_t q4w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q4w_ptr);\n            uint16_t q2w = __builtin_nontemporal_load(q2w_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack q6 into fp16x8_t\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                static uint constexpr kMask000F   = 0x000F000F;\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1024 = 0x64006400; // {1024.0, 1024.0}, fp16x2_t\n                static uint constexpr kHalf2_1056 = 0xE420E420; // {-1056.0, -1056.0}, fp16x2_t\n\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                {\n                    int32_t q4 = q4w & kMask000F;\n                    int32_t q2 = (q2w & 0x3) | ((q2w & 0xC) << 14);\n                    q4w >>= 4;\n                    q2w >>= 4;\n                    if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                    {\n                        int32_t q6 = q4 | (q2 << 4) | kHalf2_1024;\n                        asm volatile(\"v_pk_add_f16 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i])\n                                     : \"v\"(q6), \"v\"(kHalf2_1056));\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        int32_t int16_2 = q4 | (q2 << 4);\n                        int16_t low     = static_cast<int16_t>(int16_2 & 0xFFFF);\n                        int16_t high    = static_cast<int16_t>((int16_2 >> 16) & 0xFFFF);\n\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_low  = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(low));\n                        __hip_bfloat16 bf_high = __float2bfloat16(static_cast<float>(high));\n                        nv_bfloat162 bf2       = __halves2bfloat162(bf_low, bf_high);\n                        int32_t packed_bf16    = *reinterpret_cast<int32_t*>(&bf2);\n                        w[i]                   = packed_add<__hip_bfloat16>(packed_bf16, kRangeMin);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Fp8 symmetric quantization codec.\n// We quantize the FP16 data to block-scaled Fp8 in blocks of 4 *\n// kThreadGroupSize.\ntemplate <typename T, int world_size>\nstruct CodecFP8 : public CodecBase\n{\n    static int constexpr kWorldSize = world_size;\n\n    // Codec tile size process by this workgroup.\n    // Each threads processes a fragment of fp16x8_t (16B),\n    // into a fp8x8_t (8B) and a fp16 scale shared among 32 values.\n    static constexpr int kRankAtoms               = kAtoms / kWorldSize;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileStride          = 2176;\n    static constexpr int kRankTileScaleOffset     = 2048;\n    static constexpr int kRankTransmittedTileSize = kRankTileStride * kRankAtoms;\n    static_assert(kRankTransmittedTileSize % 16 == 0, \"kRankTileSize must be 16B aligned.\");\n\n    static constexpr int kRankBufferTileStride = kRankTileStride / sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n    // Total tile size for the collective communication.\n    static constexpr int kTransmittedTileSize = kRankTransmittedTileSize * kWorldSize;\n\n    // FP8 Maximum value (on AMD Instinct MI300X - float8_e4m3fnuz)\n    static float constexpr kFP8Max = 240.0f;\n    static int constexpr kScaleFactor =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x1C441C44 : 0x3B883B88; // {1/240.0h, 1/240.0h}\n    static int constexpr kScaleEpsilon =\n        std::is_same<T, half>::value ? 0x00010001 : 0x33D733D7; // {1e-7, 1e-7}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ CodecFP8(int thread, int rank) : CodecBase(thread, rank) {}\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void send(int32x4_t* __restrict__ send_buffer,\n                                            const int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t const atom = data[k];\n\n            // abs(w)\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                T const* x = reinterpret_cast<T const*>(&atom);\n                T* y       = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w);\n                for(int i = 0; i < 8; i++)\n                {\n                    y[i] = __habs(x[i]);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // max(w)\n            int wmax;\n            {\n                int a, b;\n                int* dw = reinterpret_cast<int*>(&w);\n                a       = packed_max<T>(dw[0], dw[1]);\n                b       = packed_max<T>(dw[2], dw[3]);\n                wmax    = packed_max<T>(a, b);\n\n                // Reduce the max among a group of 8 threads\n                // Note: This is basically 2 blocks of 32 values setup as the\n                // upper/lower halves of the fp16x2_t\n                for(int i = 1; i < 8; i <<= 1)\n                {\n                    int x = __shfl_down(wmax, i);\n                    wmax  = packed_max<T>(wmax, x);\n                }\n\n                // Share with the cohort\n                wmax = __shfl(wmax, group_leader);\n            }\n\n            // Derive scales\n            int decoding_scale = packed_mul<T>(wmax, kScaleFactor);\n            int encoding_scale = packed_add<T>(decoding_scale, kScaleEpsilon);\n            encoding_scale     = packed_rcp<T>(encoding_scale);\n\n            // Apply scales to get quantized values\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(atom[i], encoding_scale);\n            }\n\n            // Convert to packed FP8\n            fp32x8_t wf;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    half2 const* x = reinterpret_cast<half2 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y      = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __half22float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    nv_bfloat162 const* x = reinterpret_cast<nv_bfloat162 const*>(&w);\n                    float2* y             = reinterpret_cast<float2*>(&wf);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n                    {\n                        y[i] = __bfloat1622float2(x[i]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            int32x2_t qw;\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[0], wf[1], qw[0], 0);\n            qw[0] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[2], wf[3], qw[0], 1);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[4], wf[5], qw[1], 0);\n            qw[1] = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_fp8_f32(wf[6], wf[7], qw[1], 1);\n\n            // Write quantized atom to send_buffer\n            // note: only the group leader stores the scale\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(send_buffer + k * kRankBufferTileStride);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            __builtin_nontemporal_store(qw, qw_ptr);\n            if(threadIdx.x == group_leader)\n            {\n                __builtin_nontemporal_store(decoding_scale, qs_ptr);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    __quickreduce_device_inline__ void recv(int32x4_t** __restrict__ recv_buffer,\n                                            int32x4_t* __restrict__ data)\n    {\n        for(int k = 0; k < kRankAtoms; k++)\n        {\n            // Directly read quantized atom from recv_buffer\n            uint8_t* atom_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint8_t*>(*recv_buffer);\n            int32x2_t* qw_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x2_t*>(atom_ptr) + thread;\n            int* qs_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int*>(atom_ptr + kRankTileScaleOffset) + (thread / 8);\n\n            int32x2_t qw = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qw_ptr);\n            int qs       = __builtin_nontemporal_load(qs_ptr);\n\n            *recv_buffer += kRankBufferTileStride;\n\n            // Unpack FP8\n            int32x4_t w;\n            {\n                if constexpr(std::is_same<T, half>::value)\n                {\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1 = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 0])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf0[0]), \"v\"(wf0[1]));\n                        asm volatile(\"v_cvt_pkrtz_f16_f32 %0, %1, %2\"\n                                     : \"=v\"(w[i * 2 + 1])\n                                     : \"v\"(wf1[0]), \"v\"(wf1[1]));\n                    }\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    __hip_bfloat16* wbf = reinterpret_cast<__hip_bfloat16*>(&w);\n                    for(int i = 0; i < 2; i++)\n                    {\n                        fp32x2_t wf0_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 0);\n                        fp32x2_t wf1_vec = __builtin_amdgcn_cvt_pk_f32_fp8(qw[i], 1);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 0]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 1]   = __float2bfloat16(wf0_vec[1]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 2]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[0]);\n                        wbf[i * 4 + 3]   = __float2bfloat16(wf1_vec[1]);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Apply decoding scales\n            for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)\n            {\n                w[i] = packed_mul<T>(w[i], qs);\n            }\n\n            // That's pretty much it...\n            data[k] = w;\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n// Twoshot All Reduce\ntemplate <typename T, class Codec, bool cast_bf2half>\nstruct AllReduceTwoshot\n{\n    static_assert(sizeof(T) == 2);\n\n    static constexpr int kWorldSize = Codec::kWorldSize;\n\n    __device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                               T* __restrict__ output,\n                               uint32_t const N,                   // number of elements\n                               int const block,                    // block index\n                               int const rank,                     // rank index\n                               uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list, // communication buffers\n                               uint32_t const data_offset, // offset to start of the data buffer\n                               uint32_t flag_color,\n                               int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n    {\n        // Topology\n        int thread           = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n        uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n        Codec codec(thread, rank);\n        int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n        uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n        for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        {\n            buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Read input into registers\n        int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half)\n            {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n#pragma unroll\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j)\n                {\n                    float2 f    = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                    half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1A: Write segment data into the communication buffer of the target\n        // rank responsible for this segment.\n        uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n        uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n\n        uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = thread;\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset +\n                                                             rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n            set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n        }\n        // --------------------------------------------------------\n        // Phase-1B: Reduce the segment data from the communication buffers.\n        int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n        {\n            // Read the data from the communication buffer.\n            int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n            uint32_t* flag_ptr     = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n\n            for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n            {\n                // Wait for the flags to be set.\n                if(thread == 0)\n                {\n                    wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n                }\n                __syncthreads();\n\n                // note: we reuse tA as temp buffer here\n                codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n\n                for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                {\n                    packed_assign_add<T>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Phase-2: Write the reduced segment to every other rank\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++)\n        {\n            int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n                buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n            codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n        }\n\n        __syncthreads();\n        if(thread < kWorldSize)\n        {\n            int r              = Let me analyze the existing `AllReduceTwoshot::run` to understand the two-shot all-reduce pattern, then implement the fused version.\n\nKey observations:\n1. `kTileSize = kBlockSize * kAtoms * sizeof(int32x4_t) = 256 * 8 * 16 = 32768 bytes = 32 KiB`\n2. Each thread processes `kAtoms = 8` int32x4_t (16B each), so each thread handles 128 bytes\n3. The thread's position within the block is `thread = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront` (0-255)\n4. `kElemsPerAtom = sizeof(int32x4_t) / sizeof(T) = 16 / 2 = 8` elements per atom\n5. Each thread processes `kAtoms * kElemsPerAtom = 8 * 8 = 64` T elements\n6. The block processes `kTileSize = 32768` bytes, which is `32768 / 2 = 16384` T elements per tile\n\nFor the fused version with RMSNorm:\n- After the all-reduce completes, each thread has `tA[kAtoms]` containing the all-reduced data\n- Then add `residual_inp` to get `residual_out`\n- Then compute RMSNorm over the hidden_dim axis\n\nThe key challenge is that RMSNorm requires a reduction over `hidden_dim` elements. Since each block processes a tile of `kTileSize` bytes, and we have multiple threads per block, we need to coordinate to compute the sum of squares.\n\nLet me think about the data layout:\n- N total elements\n- hidden_dim elements per row (token)\n- N / hidden_dim total rows (tokens)\n- Each tile = kTileSize = 32768 bytes = 32K bytes\n\nFor hidden_dim=4096 bf16, each row = 4096 * 2 = 8192 bytes\nkTileSize = 32768 bytes, so 32768 / 8192 = 4 rows per tile\nThis matches the comment in the code: \"For Qwen3.5 hidden_dim=4096 bf16 rows, one 32 KiB QR tile contains four independent rows.\"\n\nFor the RMSNorm computation:\n1. Each thread has its portion of the all-reduced data in tA (plus residual)\n2. We need to compute sum of squares over hidden_dim for each row\n3. Then normalize: output = x * rsqrt(mean(x^2) + eps) * weight\n\nThe approach:\n1. After the all-reduce phase (same as AllReduceTwoshot), we have `tA[]` with the reduced values\n2. Read `residual_inp` for this block's tile, add to `tA[]`, write to `residual_out`\n3. Compute sum of squares per row across the block (using shared memory / warp shuffles)\n4. Apply RMSNorm formula\n\nLet me think more carefully about the data layout within a tile. The tile layout is:\n- Block processes `kTileSize = 256 * 8 * 16 = 32768` bytes\n- Thread `thread` handles atoms at offsets: `thread * sizeof(int32x4_t)` = `thread * 16` bytes for atom 0, `(thread + kBlockSize) * 16` for atom 1, etc.\n\nSo the data layout is interleaved across threads:\n- Atom 0: thread 0 is at byte 0, thread 1 at byte 16, ..., thread 255 at byte 4080\n- Atom 1: thread 0 at byte 4096, thread 1 at byte 4112, ...\n- ...\n- Atom 7: thread 0 at byte 28672, thread 1 at byte 28688, ...\n\nEach atom holds `kElemsPerAtom = 8` T elements (8 * 2 = 16 bytes).\n\nSo one tile has:\n- Total T elements per tile: `kTileSize / sizeof(T) = 32768 / 2 = 16384`\n\nFor hidden_dim=4096 and bf16 (sizeof(T)=2):\n- row_bytes = 4096 * 2 = 8192\n- rows_per_tile = kTileSize / row_bytes = 32768 / 8192 = 4\n\nEach row within the tile is `row_bytes = 8192` bytes, which is `8192 / 16 = 512` atoms = `512 / kBlockSize = 2` atoms worth of data per thread contribution to a row. Wait, let me re-think.\n\nActually, within a tile:\n- Total bytes: 32768\n- Bytes per row: 8192\n- Rows per tile: 4\n\nThe kAtoms for one tile is 8. Of these 8 atoms worth of data, each atom stride spans kBlockSize = 256 positions. So:\n- positions 0-255 (atoms 0) span bytes 0-4095 (the first 2048 T elements = first half of first two rows or...)\n\nWait, let me think about this differently. The tile processes kTileSize = 32768 bytes.\n\nThe layout in memory for the tile:\n- Thread 0 reads: bytes [0, 16) (atom 0), bytes [4096, 4112) (atom 1), ..., bytes [28672, 28688) (atom 7)\n- Thread 1 reads: bytes [16, 32) (atom 0), bytes [4112, 4128) (atom 1), ...\n\nSo the first 256 atoms (by thread index) cover bytes 0-4095 for atom 0, then 4096-8191 for atom 1, etc.\n\nActually, let me reconsider. The src_offset is:\n```\nsrc_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n```\nand then:\n```\nsrc_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n```\nwhere kAtomStride = kBlockSize = 256.\n\nSo thread reads at offsets from block*tile_start:\n- atom 0: thread * 16\n- atom 1: (thread + 256) * 16\n- ...\n- atom 7: (thread + 7*256) * 16\n\nThe total number of elements in a tile: 32768/2 = 16384 T elements.\nPer thread: kAtoms * kElemsPerAtom = 8 * 8 = 64 T elements.\n\nNow for hidden_dim=4096:\n- Each row has 4096 elements = 8192 bytes\n- Per tile: 16384 / 4096 = 4 rows\n- Row occupies 8192 bytes / 16 bytes_per_atom = 512 positions in the tile\n\nThe positions at which thread data falls:\n- atom 0, byte offset = thread * 16. This is position thread in the \"atom layout\"\n- For T elements (2 bytes each), thread 0 reads elements 0-7 at atom 0, then elements starting at position 256*8=2048 at atom 1, etc.\n\nSo the first row (elements 0-4095) covers:\n- atoms 0 and 1 fully (threads 0-255 at atom 0 gives elements 0-2047, threads 0-255 at atom 1 gives elements 2048-4095)\n- Wait no. Atom 0 starts at byte 0. Thread 0 reads bytes [0, 16), containing 8 elements (0-7). Thread 1 reads bytes [16, 32), elements 8-15. ... Thread 255 reads bytes [4080, 4096), elements 2040-2047. So atom 0 covers elements 0-2047 (the first 2048 elements = first 4096 bytes).\n- Atom 1 starts at byte 4096 (= 256*16). Thread 0 reads bytes [4096, 4112), elements 2048-2055. Thread 255 reads bytes [8176, 8192), elements 4088-4095. So atom 1 covers elements 2048-4095 (the next 2048 elements).\n\nSo atoms 0+1 = one full row of 4096 elements. And atoms 2+3 = second row, atoms 4+5 = third row, atoms 6+7 = fourth row.\n\nSo each pair of consecutive atoms covers one row. Within each pair:\n- The first atom gives the first half of the row (elements [0, 2048) of the row)\n- The second atom gives the second half (elements [2048, 4096))\n\nAnd within each atom, thread `t` holds elements `[t*8, t*8+8)` of that half-row.\n\nNow for RMSNorm, we need to compute sum of squares over the hidden_dim=4096 elements for each of the 4 rows.\n\nAfter the all-reduce, each thread has `tA[0..7]` containing 8 atoms, where atoms (2i, 2i+1) belong to row i.\n\nTo compute the RMSNorm, we need:\n1. For each row, compute sum of squares of all hidden_dim elements\n2. The sum requires coordination across all 256 threads (since each thread holds 64 elements of the 4096)\n\nThis is a classic block reduction pattern. We can use shared memory for this.\n\nHere's my plan for the implementation:\n\n```cpp\n__device__ static void run(...) {\n    // 1. Same all-reduce as AllReduceTwoshot (Phases 1 and 2)\n    // 2. During or after receiving data, add residual_inp \n    // 3. Write residual_out\n    // 4. Compute row-wise sum of squares\n    // 5. Block reduction to get per-row means\n    // 6. Normalize and write output\n    \n    int thread = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n    uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n    Codec codec(thread, rank);\n    int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n    uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n    for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i) {\n        buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n    }\n    \n    // Read input into registers\n    int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n    BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n    uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    for(int i = 0; The kernel has:\n- tA[kAtoms] = 8 * 4 = 32 int registers (each int32x4_t is 4 ints)\n- tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = 4 * 4 = 16 int registers (for FP codec with world_size=2, kRankAtoms=4)\n- Total: 48 registers just for the data\n\nPlus the loop variables, flags, buffer descriptors, etc. The `__launch_bounds__(256, 4)` hint tells the compiler to limit register usage to fit 4 blocks per CUs. Each CU has 65536 VGPRs (on MI300), so per block: 65536 / 4 = 16384 VGPRs. With 256 threads per block: 16384 / 256 = 64 VGPRs per thread. 48 VGPRs for data + overhead ≈ 60 VGPRs, which should fit.\n\nActually, after Phase 2, tR[] is no longer needed. So during the RMSNorm phase, we only need tA[] (32 registers). That's fine.\n\nAlright, I'm definitely ready to write the code now. Let me structure it cleanly:\n\n```cpp\n__device__ static void run(T const* __restrict__ input,\n                           T const* __restrict__ residual_inp,\n                           T* __restrict__ residual_out,\n                           T* __restrict__ output,\n                           T const* __restrict__ weight,\n                           float eps,\n                           uint32_t const N,\n                           uint32_t const hidden_dim,\n                           int const block,\n                           int const rank,\n                           uint8_t** __restrict__ buffer_list,\n                           uint32_t const data_offset,\n                           uint32_t flag_color,\n                           int64_t data_size_per_phase)\n{\n    // ---- Setup ----\n    int thread           = threadIdx.x + threadIdx.y * kWavefront;\n    uint8_t* rank_buffer = buffer_list[rank];\n    Codec codec(thread, rank);\n    int block_id = blockIdx.x;\n    uint8_t* buffer_ptr[kWorldSize];\n    for(int i = 0; i < kWorldSize; ++i)\n        buffer_ptr[i] = buffer_list[i];\n\n    // ---- Read input ----\n    int32x4_t tA[kAtoms];\n    {\n        BufferResource src_buffer(const_cast<T*>(input), N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t src_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++)\n        {\n            tA[i] = buffer_load_dwordx4(src_buffer.descriptor, src_offset, 0, 0);\n            src_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n            if constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n                const nv_bfloat162* bf_buf = reinterpret_cast<const nv_bfloat162*>(&tA[i]);\n                half2 half_buf[4];\n                for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                    float2 f = __bfloat1622float2(bf_buf[j]);\n                    half_buf[j] = __float22half2_rn(f);\n                }\n                tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(half_buf);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---- Phase 1A: Send ----\n    uint32_t comm_data0_offset = data_offset + block_id * Codec::kTransmittedTileSize;\n    uint32_t comm_data1_offset = data_size_per_phase + comm_data0_offset;\n    uint32_t comm_flags0_offset = block_id * (kWorldSize * sizeof(uint32_t));\n    uint32_t comm_flags1_offset = (data_offset / 2) + comm_flags0_offset;\n\n    for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n        int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data0_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n        codec.send(send_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n    }\n    __syncthreads();\n    if(thread < kWorldSize) {\n        int r = thread;\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags0_offset + rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n    }\n\n    // ---- Phase 1B: Reduce ----\n    int32x4_t tR[Codec::kRankAtoms] = {};\n    {\n        int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data0_offset);\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags0_offset);\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n            if(thread == 0)\n                wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n            __syncthreads();\n            codec.recv(&recv_buffer, tA);\n            for(int i = 0; i < Codec::kRankAtoms; i++)\n                packed_assign_add<CommT>(&tR[i], &tA[i]);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---- Phase 2: Scatter reduced + Gather ----\n    for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n        int32x4_t* send_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_data1_offset + rank * Codec::kRankTransmittedTileSize);\n        codec.send(send_buffer, tR);\n    }\n    __syncthreads();\n    if(thread < kWorldSize) {\n        int r = thread;\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(\n            buffer_ptr[r] + comm_flags1_offset + rank * sizeof(uint32_t));\n        set_sync_flag(flag_ptr, flag_color);\n    }\n    {\n        int32x4_t* recv_buffer = reinterpret_cast<int32x4_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_data1_offset);\n        uint32_t* flag_ptr = reinterpret_cast<uint32_t*>(rank_buffer + comm_flags1_offset);\n        for(int r = 0; r < kWorldSize; r++) {\n            if(thread == 0)\n                wait_sync_flag(&flag_ptr[r], flag_color);\n            __syncthreads();\n            codec.recv(&recv_buffer, &tA[r * Codec::kRankAtoms]);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---- Cast CommT → T if needed (cast_bf2half: CommT=half → T=bf16) ----\n    if constexpr(cast_bf2half) {\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n            const half2* half_buf = reinterpret_cast<const half2*>(&tA[i]);\n            nv_bfloat162 bf16_buf[4];\n            for(int j = 0; j < 4; ++j) {\n                float2 f = __half22float2(half_buf[j]);\n                bf16_buf[j] = __float22bfloat162_rn(f);\n            }\n            tA[i] = *reinterpret_cast<const int32x4_t*>(bf16_buf);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ---- Read residual, add, write residual_out ----\n    // At this point tA[] is in T precision\n    {\n        BufferResource res_buffer(const_cast<T*>(residual_inp), N * sizeof(T));\n        BufferResource res_out_buffer(residual_out, N * sizeof(T));\n        uint32_t byte_offset = block * kTileSize + thread * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        for(int i = 0; i < kAtoms; i++) {\n            int32x4_t res_val = buffer_load_dwordx4(res_buffer.descriptor, byte_offset, 0, 0);\n            packed_assign_add<T>(&tA[i], &res_val);\n            buffer_store_dwordx4(tA[i], res_out_buffer.descriptor, byte_offset, 0, 0);\n            byte_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // tA[] now = all_reduced + residual = residual_out values (in T precision)\n    \n    // ---- RMSNorm ----\n    // Compute per-row sums of squares, then normalize\n    constexpr uint32_t kElemPerAtomTotal = kBlockSize * kElemsPerAtom; // 2048\n    uint32_t atoms_per_row = hidden_dim / kElemPerAtomTotal;\n    uint32_t rows_per_tile = kAtoms / atoms_per_row;\n\n    __shared__ float smem_reduce[kBlockSize / kWavefront]; // 4 floats\n\n    int warp_id = threadIdx.y;  // 0..3\n    int lane_id = threadIdx.x;  // 0..63\n\n    // Weight buffer\n    BufferResource w_buffer(const_cast<T*>(weight), hidden_dim * sizeof(T));\n    BufferResource out_buffer(output, N * sizeof(T));\n\n    for(uint32_t row = 0; row < rows_per_tile; row++) {\n        // Partial sum of squares for this row\n        float partial_sq = 0.0f;\n        uint32_t base_atom = row * atoms_per_row;\n        for(uint32_t j = 0; j < atoms_per_row; j++) {\n            T* elems = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[base_atom + j]);\n            for(int k = 0; k < kElemsPerAtom; k++) {\n                float v = qr_to_float(elems[k]);\n                partial_sq += v * v;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Warp-level reduction\n        for(int s = 1; s < kWavefront; s <<= 1)\n            partial_sq += __shfl_down(partial_sq, s);\n\n        // Cross-warp reduction via shared memory\n        if(lane_id == 0)\n            smem_reduce[warp_id] = partial_sq;\n        __syncthreads();\n\n        float total_sq;\n        if(thread == 0) {\n            total_sq = 0.0f;\n            for(int w = 0; w < kBlockSize / kWavefront; w++)\n                total_sq += smem_reduce[w];\n        }\n        __syncthreads();\n        \n        // Hmm wait, I need to be more careful. thread == 0 lane_id=0, warp_id=0.\n        // But I want all threads to have total_sq for the normalization.\n        // Let me use a different approach.\n    }\n}\n```\n\nOK I'm going to take a different approach for the broadcast. Let me compute total_sq on thread 0, store to smem_reduce[0], and have all threads read it.\n\n```cpp\n// Cross-warp reduction\nif(lane_id == 0)\n    smem_reduce[warp_id] = partial_sq;\n__syncthreads();\n\nif(thread == 0) {\n    float total = 0.0f;\n    for(int w = 0; w < 4; w++)\n        total += smem_reduce[w];\n    smem_reduce[0] = total;\n}\n__syncthreads();\n\nfloat total_sq = smem_reduce[0];\nfloat variance = total_sq * (1.0f / static_cast<float>(hidden_dim)) + eps;\nfloat denom = rsqrtf(variance);\n```\n\nWait, but I have a subtle issue here. During the first `__syncthreads()`, all threads need to have written their warp sums. But only lane_id == 0 writes. The other threads in each warp are idle. After __syncthreads(), smem_reduce[0..3] have the warp sums. Thread 0 reads all 4 and sums them, stores to smem_reduce[0]. Then __syncthreads() and all threads read smem_reduce[0].\n\nActually, there's a problem with `__shfl_down` in a wavefront. On AMD GPU, each wavefront is 64 threads. The block has 4 wavefronts, arranged as dim3(64, 4, 1). So threadIdx.x = lane within wavefront (0-63), threadIdx.y = wavefront (0-3). The hardware warp is 64 threads, so each thread (tx, ty) belongs to warp `ty`.\n\n`__shfl_down(val, stride)` operates within the current warp (64 threads). So the warp-level reduction `for(int s = 1; s < 64; s <<= 1) val += __shfl_down(val, s)` correctly reduces within each warp.\n\nAfter that, Lane 0 of each warp (tx=0, ty=w) has the warp sum. These 4 values are stored in smem_reduce[0..3]. Then thread (0,0) (the global thread 0) sums them.\n\nThis looks correct. Let me also make sure the __syncthreads() calls are in the right places:\n\n1. After writing smem_reduce[warp_id] (by lane 0 of each warp): __syncthreads() ensures all 4 values are written before thread 0 reads.\n2. After thread 0 writes smem_reduce[0]: __syncthreads() ensures all threads see the final value.\n\nYes, this is correct. But wait, I have TWO __syncthreads() in sequence for each row. For 4 rows, that's 8 __syncthreads(). This is fine for correctness but adds some overhead. Since we're already doing a full block reduction, the overhead is probably dominated by the reduction itself.\n\nActually, I just realized that rows_per_tile is at most kAtoms = 8 (when atoms_per_row = 1, i.e., hidden_dim = 2048). For larger hidden_dim, it's fewer rows. For the test case (hidden_dim = 4096, bf16), rows_per_tile = 4. So we have 4 iterations, each with 2 __syncthreads. Total: 8 __syncthreads. This should be fine.\n\nNow, let me think about the weight load. For each row, for each atom j, I load 8 weight values. Then I compute output = x * denom * weight and store to output.\n\n```cpp\nfor(uint32_t row = 0; row < rows_per_tile; row++) {\n    // ... reduction to get denom ...\n\n    // Normalize and write output\n    uint32_t base_atom = row * atoms_per_row;\n    // Weight byte offset for this row's portion\n    // For atom j, thread: weight offset = (j * kBlockSize + thread) * sizeof(int32x4_t)\n    uint32_t w_byte_offset = thread * sizeof(int32x4_t); // starts at j=0\n    uint32_t out_byte_offset = block * kTileSize + (base_atom * kBlockSize + thread) * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    \n    for(uint32_t j = 0; j < atoms_per_row; j++) {\n        T* elems = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&tA[base_atom + j]);\n        \n        int32x4_t w_val = buffer_load_dwordx4(w_buffer.descriptor, w_byte_offset, 0, 0);\n        T* w_elems = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&w_val);\n        \n        int32x4_t out_val;\n        T* out_elems = reinterpret_cast<T*>(&out_val);\n        for(int k = 0; k < kElemsPerAtom; k++) {\n            float x = qr_to_float(elems[k]);\n            float w = qr_to_float(w_elems[k]);\n            out_elems[k] = qr_from_float<T>(x * denom * w);\n        }\n        \n        buffer_store_dwordx4(out_val, out_buffer.descriptor, out_byte_offset, 0, 0);\n        \n        w_byte_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n        out_byte_offset += kAtomStride * sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nWait, let me check w_byte_offset for j=1:\n- j=0: w_byte_offset = thread * 16\n- j=1: w_byte_offset = thread * 16 + 256 * 16 = (256 + thread) * 16\n\nThis corresponds to weight indices (256 + thread) * 8 through (256 + thread) * 8 + 7. For hidden_dim = 4096 (atoms_per_row = 2), these are indices [2048 + thread*8, 2048 + thread*8+8), which is the second half of the row's weight. ✓\n\nAnd the output byte offset for j=1:\n- base_atom = row * 2, j = 1, atom_idx = row * 2 + 1\n- out_byte_offset = block * kTileSize + ((row * 2 + 1) * 256 + thread) * 16\n\nThis writes to the correct position in the output. ✓\n\nOne more thing: the tA[] data for the RMSNorm. After adding residual and storing to residual_out, tA[row * atoms_per_row + j] contains the residual_out data for that atom. The elements in tA[] represent the same data that we need for the RMSNorm normalization. I need to be very careful and not miss anything. I'll write it section by section.\n\nWait, actually I need to think about one more performance aspect. The `buffer_load_dwordx4` for reading residual and weight will go through HBM. For the residual read, it's the same amount of data as the unfused path. For the weight, it's the same.\n\nBut there's a potential issue: the residual and weight loads happen after the communication phase, which means there might be latency hiding opportunities. In the unfused path, the QR kernel writes output to HBM, then the RMSNorm kernel reads from HBM. In the fused path, after communication, we read residual and weight. Since the communication round-trip finishes before we start the RMSNorm, and the HBM reads for residual/weight can overlap with other work (if we use software pipelining), the performance should be OK.\n\nFor a first implementation, I'll keep it simple without software pipelining. The correctness is more important, and the 2% threshold should be achievable by just avoiding the HBM round-trip of the all-reduced tensor.\n\nOK, final code:\n\nActually, I realize there's a subtle issue. Good.\n\nBut wait, when CommT = half, a zero-initialized int32x4_t has all bits = 0. In half precision, 0x0000 = 0.0.
